    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3043699930" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer674367137136115324">This is going to sound really stupid, but I recently got a puppy and I found the new level of responsibly extremely stressful. It changed so much about my life that I began to doubt my ability not only to care for my puppy, but to be able to handle all other aspects of my life. But after a great success using </span>
  <span id="freeText674367137136115324" style="display:none">This is going to sound really stupid, but I recently got a puppy and I found the new level of responsibly extremely stressful. It changed so much about my life that I began to doubt my ability not only to care for my puppy, but to be able to handle all other aspects of my life. I felt like a complete failure and needed a boost, and not just the temporary one that chocolate brings.<br /><br />I'm fairly new to the world of self-help books, having read the odd one in the past. But after a great success using a self-help book to help me beat my fear of flying and get on a place for the first time in 20 years, I'm much more open to them. 'Stepping Beyond Intention' by Daniel Mangena seemed like it would give me the advice and tools I needed to get past the block I had put on myself and help me to deal with some of my anxieties. And it really did!<br /><br />The focus on 'Stepping Beyond Intention' is working on your own personal growth. By talking about his own experiences, I was reminded that in my past I have too struggled, but I came out of the other side every time, and this time I would too. Instead of providing you with a few motivational quotes, you are actually given tools and techniques to grow, however, you may need to. A very useful read for me.<br /></span>

<div id="review_2959261648" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2959261648" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2959261648?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2959261648" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16850513053515121599">‘Quit complaining – make yourself a magnet for more positive experiences’<br/><br/>British author Daniel Mangena formed The Mangena Foundation in 2015 and incorporated England and Wales in 2017 as a non-profit organization whose mission is to empower the next generations to create a better, brighter, safer, and more loving world. The foundation builds schools and orphanage in third world countries, mentors children in foster care and children’s homes in the UK and mentors young offenders and those in the </span>
  <span id="freeText16850513053515121599" style="display:none">‘Quit complaining – make yourself a magnet for more positive experiences’<br /><br />British author Daniel Mangena formed The Mangena Foundation in 2015 and incorporated England and Wales in 2017 as a non-profit organization whose mission is to empower the next generations to create a better, brighter, safer, and more loving world. The foundation builds schools and orphanage in third world countries, mentors children in foster care and children’s homes in the UK and mentors young offenders and those in the criminal justice system in the UK. The key phrases are ‘emancipation through education’, ‘a safe home for every child’, ‘teaching creative independence’, and ‘supporting the value of creators of tomorrow.’ <br /><br />In this exceptional book, Daniel’s mission statement carries impact: “Spearhead an evolutionary uplift in universal consciousness by awakening people to the importance of their unique role. This that is already encoded in them by way of a deep and often ignored or undervalued passion defined as their Dream.” And as he has stated before, ‘Growth is a key component in nature—if you aren’t growing you are dying.’ His gift: a four-step system now called the Beyond Intention Paradigm. <br /><br />As is his charge, Daniel focuses on guiding us on personal growth – the important step to taking control of our lives and fulfilling our dreams. In his words, ‘If you look at every experience that has been in your life, there is only one thing that has been present there all the time; you. In every win. In every lesson. In every challenge. You. This simple truth came to me at a truly dark time. If was this recognition that pulled me back from the brink of taking my own life; I was there at the centre of every experience I had sought to escape. If I change me, I can change it all. That moment was the birth of Beyond Intention and the start of my journey into my true purpose here on earth, and was born in a situation where I had every reason to push blame in a 100 different directions. But the joy I have in my life today, stems directly from my owning this.’<br /><br />Perhaps the most pertinent view of the importance of this book is Daniel’s statement as follows: ‘Step with me Beyond Intention and open your mind to the paradigm of pure intention made manifest in your life, deliberately on command each time. I am not a scientist or mystic or sage but spent some time in the mystery schools and have spent nearly 20 years at the feet of all three of the former. I am a student of such, just as we are all students of life. I will not therefore insult the great works of others living and passed on who have dedicated themselves to teaching some of the more specialized areas that I will be sharing with you in this book. As much as possible I will be directing you to additional resources to add depth and substance to the ideas explored in this introductory journey into my work, but I do in all instances ask for your patience where certain leaps are made and do invite you to look a little deeper before rejecting any concepts that I have not expounded on with the greatest elegance.’ <br /><br />With that degree of supportive guidance and compassion, Daniel shares his life experiences that provide the foundation upon which we can implement our growth into enriched lives. Very highly recommended. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16850513053515121599" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2983012514" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2983012514" />
    <a title="Dionysos" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/102973684-dionysos"><img alt="Dionysos" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568901577p2/102973684.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2983012514?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dionysos" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dionysos" href="/user/show/102973684-dionysos">Dionysos</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2983012514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3190354066758885426">UK author Daniel Mangena starts off his book here with admitting that he is not a scientist or mystic or sage but has gained much of his knowledge and insights from the school called life as we all learn about everything from it by what we go through and what we encounter. Mangena tells us that through this book, we will be learning how to direct our lives by choosing “here and now” paths that connect with the desired results that we all want to gain in life. Mangena further states that if we co</span>
  <span id="freeText3190354066758885426" style="display:none">UK author Daniel Mangena starts off his book here with admitting that he is not a scientist or mystic or sage but has gained much of his knowledge and insights from the school called life as we all learn about everything from it by what we go through and what we encounter. Mangena tells us that through this book, we will be learning how to direct our lives by choosing “here and now” paths that connect with the desired results that we all want to gain in life. Mangena further states that if we consider all the experiences that we have gone through, we will come to realize that the “only thing that has been present through it all is: us.” He tells us that we are the key figures through all the times we win, we learn a lesson, and in every challenge that we face.” Throughout this book, Mangena talks about his paradigm that he calls, “Beyond Intention”, which is a system of steps, tools and knowledge that he believes will help those who take part in it achieve their full potentials, attaining happiness, successes and the like. Also, Mangena informs us the readers that “Beyond Intention” is “structured to ‘reprogram the operating system that we manage so that there will be no need to focus on the conscious’ exceeding of the unconscious programs in us for they are all operating side by side for our supreme goodness.” Near the end of this intriguing book, Mangena is said to have initially developed “Beyond Intention” as a lifeline for his overwhelming suicidal thoughts. This basic, 4-step process really ended up turning his misery to happiness and as a result, making him want to share it with the world to which the full “Beyond Intention” system came into fruition.<br /><br />This is an interesting, intriguing, but exceptional work because there are some grammatical drawbacks here and there but all in all, Mangena comes through as positive and very devoted to his creation, the Beyond Intention paradigm. He gives some great points and easily seems to describe his system in great detail. Mangena does give instances of when he was feeling low and depressive and how he utilizes his program every now and then to erase the feelings of doubt and negativity that may rise. I found this book to be an easy-to-read experience as well as a short and detailed book that all who may decide to read it may comprehend and understand.<br /><br />I recommend this book to the depressed soul who has tried but to no avail therapy and any other psychological assistance there is out there. Just give this guy’s “Beyond Intention” some of your time and who knows, maybe it will work for you. Mangena lists all of his social media links and websites at the end of this book so that you can try him and his help out for your depression or suicidal thoughts. I think it works for the reluctant reader for it is only a 100 or less pages in length. I read this on kindle so it went by so fast and I was able to complete in three days long. I know it could be shorter for you, who knows?<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3190354066758885426" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Written as more of a handbook with a description of a person's state of being in a given situation and how to best handle yourself.   <span id="freeText7558204525824015936" style="display:none">Stepping Beyond Intention illuminates and demands full concentration.<br />Metaphysical education will help follow your heart, mind and soul on a conscious and subconscious level. Written as more of a handbook with a description of a person's state of being in a given situation and how to best handle yourself. If you are angry, breathe deeply, focus on the emotion and throw away the toxicity.<br /><br />You are not in balance with the Earth and the energies that surround your life bring difficulty, strife and chaos. Daniel Mangena teaches how to embody self-worth, self-care and deep meditation that flows outward. Some may not respond to these methods but this is Eastern philosophy at its finest.<br />Handle life's problems with questions of logic over emotion. Meditate through what you are feeling so the answers of logic flow naturally to your organs.<br />4 step process to better attention and commitment towards personal growth. Resolve struggles through understanding, empathy and bravery instead of anger, mistreatment and strife.<br /><br />Beyond Intention is a University course and there is an inclusion for the syllabus in the book associated to a link.<br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('M9HqSMB3Gw6RyAugFIoCqMETViba2v9Qih0XFpVuoD507+CgnImz1kLDCTf/iTc5u/cUfhzKCnCWb1azkBaEew==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EFpymWLg4trxkm7/Y2prgRHAS7mWLtMK/IRaU8LJOQdXZHhxPh5KAiKZbGiIaV4QayQJ4VA+Jirg9hv2x7EdQg==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/17992633.Daniel_Mangena">About Daniel Mangena</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/17992633.Daniel_Mangena"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1535260488p3/17992633.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13772149553533796253"><br/>After receiving a late diagnosis of Asperger’s and experiencing what can only be described as life-shattering trauma at the age of just 20, Daniel spent the next seven years struggling to keep these revelations and events from spilling into every area and aspect of his life. As a result of his own personal struggles, Daniel has built a simple, four-step system now called the Beyond Intention Parad</span>
  <span id="freeText13772149553533796253" style="display:none"><br />After receiving a late diagnosis of Asperger’s and experiencing what can only be described as life-shattering trauma at the age of just 20, Daniel spent the next seven years struggling to keep these revelations and events from spilling into every area and aspect of his life. As a result of his own personal struggles, Daniel has built a simple, four-step system now called the Beyond Intention Paradigm. <br /><br />Daniel initially built Beyond Intention as a lifeline while he grappled with suicidal thoughts and ideation. But as he transformed his life from misery to celebration, Daniel realized he could help others do the same, and thus Beyond Intention was born. Through his own struggles, Daniel found a path to lasting joy and purpose in his life, and he wants nothing more than to share the tools that saved his life. To that end, he lives by this mission statement: <br /><br />“Spearhead an evolutionary uplift in universal consciousness by awakening people to the importance of their unique role. This that is already encoded in them by way of a deep and often ignored or undervalued passion defined as their Dream.”<br /><br />Through motivational speech, Daniel shares his vision of empowerment and joy, as well as through books he has authored, his Do it With Dan” podcast series (which is available on all major platforms), frequent blogging, articles, and a series of worldwide workshops. On top of all this, Daniel offers coaching and consultations in groups and in one-on-one sessions. Each of these sessions aims to honor his mission and help his clients find the meaning and joy in their lives, just as he did. <br /><br />Daniel is also a voracious reader, publicly documenting his challenge to read a book every week. He loves to travel, writes and performs as a singer-songwriter, and practices various martial arts (Tai Chi, Brazilian Jujitsu) and meditation. Besides his own endeavours, he is an outspoken promoter of entrepreneurial philanthropy, as well as an ambassador for the Mangena Foundation. He also works with several charities across the globe and considers himself a patron of many. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13772149553533796253" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
